- section: tour
- type: multi_day
- title: 11-Day Morocco Desert Tour from Marrakech
- category: Tours from Marrakech
- location: Marrakech, Morocco
- overview: |
    This 11-day Morocco desert tour from Marrakech is a private grand loop to the Sahara dunes of Merzouga, led by knowledgeable desert guides and local drivers who know the Sahara well. The route crosses the Atlas Mountains and follows the Dades and Todra Gorges on the way to our Sahara camp, then loops north through Fes, Chefchaouen and Rabat. If you prefer a shorter Sahara escape, see our 3-day Sahara desert tour from Marrakech or request a tailor-made quote.
- highlights:
    - Arrival to Marrakech Transfer
    - Marrakech city and medina guided tour
    - Atlas Mountains and Aït Benhaddou
    - Ouarzazate, Dades and Todra Gorges
    - Private driver-guide
- duration: 11 days
- group_size: 
- age_range: 
- base_price: 
- languages: English, French, Spanish
- included:
    - Transfers from/to the airport/hotels
    - Private transportation in a spacious, air-conditioned vehicle
    - Experienced local tour guide
    - All dinners and breakfasts
    - Overnight stays in hotels, riads and desert camp
    - Desert guide and camel trek in Merzouga
- excluded:
    - Lunches and soft drinks
    - Admission fees and gratuities
- itinerary:
    - Day 1: Arrival in Marrakech and transfer to your hotel
    - Day 2: Marrakech City and Medina Guided Tour
    - Day 3: Marrakech, Atlas Mountains, Aït Benhaddou and Ouarzazate
    - Day 4: Ouarzazate, Dades Gorges, Todra Gorges, Erfoud and Merzouga
    - Day 5: Merzouga Erfoud Ziz Valley Midelt Fes
    - Day 6: Guided Tour of Fes
    - Day 7: Fes Ouazane Chefchaouen
    - Day 8: Chefchaouen
    - Day 9: Chefchaouen to Rabat via Tangier and Asilah
    - Day 10: Rabat, Casablanca and Marrakech
    - Day 11: Transfer to the airport

- section: tour
- type: multi_day
- title: 2 Days Fes to Sahara Desert & Back
- category: Tours from Fes
- location: Fes, Morocco
- overview: |
